1)
Our Position Viewed from the Providential Course
I have received a comprehensive report on the results of your hard work so far. 
So, I would like to say a word about the period leading up to this conference.
Historical Background of the Second Seven-Year Course
As you know, the second seven-year course is set to end in 1974. However, we have based this on the solar calendar, starting from April 1975, but from the original meaningful perspective, we have included the lunar calendar and established the boundary line of providence. Therefore, the providential view we had to overcome during the second seven-year course was how to lay the foundation to surpass national standards by that time.
Because of this, the second seven-year course, where the Israelite people failed to establish the foundation centered on Jesus 2,000 years ago, must be restored through indemnity. From this conclusive perspective, we see that Jesus could not unite with the rulers of that nation and the Jewish community. The three could not become one. Due to this tragic fate, the historical providence has been extended.
Furthermore, because of this, the Israelite people have become a miserable fallen nation, and we know that they have become a nation that has undergone physical indemnity in world history.
June 16, 1975 (Monday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This speech was given at a national ministers' meeting, and the title was added by the editor.
8   Our Position Viewed from the Providential Course
Because of the mistake of the Israelite people, it is natural that the Israelite people have undergone physical indemnity for 2,000 years. However, even Christianity, which has continued the foundation of spiritual salvation providence, had to face persecution regarding both physical and spiritual issues. We have come to this point while being subjected to Satan's offensive against the spiritual foundation based on the physical.
Thus, having gone through 2,000 years of history, from the individual to the family, nation, and world, we have established a new religious nation centered on the United States, which has laid a victorious foundation to move a new spiritual world. From this perspective, what kind of nation is the United States? From that viewpoint, it is a nation that has borne fruit as a result of the sacrifices of Christianity centered on the spirit and flesh. Because the United States is such a nation, we cannot help but think about how God's providence will integrate this Christianity.
Because Christianity was scattered worldwide due to Jesus, in the future era of unification, when Jesus fulfills His will, this must be reorganized; otherwise, all the merits of Jesus' death will be scattered. Therefore, we must bind this together and connect the foundation of the spiritual world to heaven. You know this is the providential view, and the teacher also understands this well. Despite this providential view...
The confrontation between the Unification Church and Christianity in Korea is not limited to this Korean peninsula. What this means is that it is historical on a global scale. Moreover, when viewed from the perspective of providence, it cannot be anything other than the origin of the confrontation between Satan and God. The Unification Church has entered into such a tragic, historically miserable fate due to being opposed on Korean soil.
Therefore, we must sacrifice our position in this process. We must restore through indemnity. The Unification Church has taken 1960 as its starting point for this. Thus, it is believed that the second seven-year course ended on May 10 of this year, based on a standard of 21 years. Then, how does the Unification Church, based on 1960, surpass national standards in Korea over the 14 years? This is the providential view that the teacher sees, and to surpass this, we must have a foundation that can absorb the Christian world. Without that foundation, we cannot surpass this; this is the principled perspective.
The Path of Destiny the Unification Church Must Take
So, from an internal perspective, how have I led the Unification Church so far? It has been to restore the indemnity of Christianity centered on spirit and flesh. In the physical aspect, the Israelite people have paid the price of blood and sacrifice, representing many nations. Until the establishment of the government in 1948, events centered around Germany unfolded. Why did such results occur? It is because the Jews did not reach the limit of physical indemnity in world history. This is God's whip that must be filled with blood, and it is Satan's final decisive blow.
Because of the price of such sacrifice, the teacher started with the victory on the heavenly side of World War II. At that time, what was the position of the Republic of Korea? There was no nation. There was no nation. During that time, who stood in the leading position? It was those who had come into contact with Western civilization. As you know, those who participated in this regime (the Lee regime) were precisely such people. During such times, the teacher started alone on Korean soil. Thus, in order to prepare for a certain time, I went through the path of gathering spiritual groups, and I critically analyzed the state of faith in Korea. Because I knew how to discern the leading direction for the future, I conveyed all such intentions to the so-called prominent figures in Korea.
From that perspective, in order for heaven to fulfill this intention, many intermediate organizations needed to be prepared in the Republic of Korea, and although such organizations came out according to God's will, the results all returned in failure. Consequently, the established churches themselves condemned such spiritual groups as Satan's work. There were many organizations prepared through such an environment, and the teacher tried to connect these organizations in a comprehensive manner, but they all disappeared because they did not understand the internal circumstances of heaven from a flat perspective, and only the Unification Church remained, confronting the established churches, bearing all the persecutions that past spiritual organizations had suffered until now.
If you find something strange here, it might be the question of why, instead of fighting back and seeking legal redress when persecuted, we just endured. This is because the original intention of the restoration providence is to reveal justice through the operation of taking back what is rightfully ours. Therefore, I quietly worked to build a foundation from the individual level to the family level.
As mentioned earlier, due to the opposition from the established churches, the urgent issue was to form a single sect in place of the established churches. Before Judaism, Jesus did not die but instead established a form of Christianity centered on Jesus to replace Judaism, which had to influence the Jewish people. If we had surpassed Judaism and held hands with the Roman Empire, there would have been a way to survive. Similarly, today, the Unification Church must take such a path of destiny; this is the principled perspective. Therefore, we had to gather young people and establish a new denomination.

Now, how should we lead the Unification Church? However, the Unification Church is not unable to go its way just because they have passed through. The new stage of education and its goals in the Unification Church

The training consists of a 3-week training program, which is officially conducted. After the 3-week training is completed, the next step is a 40-day training, followed by a 120-day training. This process is currently being implemented officially.

All members of the Unification Church around the world must go through the 120-day training process, regardless of who they are. After completing the 120-day training, everyone must engage in public life for at least 3 years.

The title I want to speak about today is "Heirs." I would like to share a few thoughts on this topic.

The reality has more conditions of unhappiness than happiness.

Whether it is individuals, families, nations, or the world, people are hoping for something. If we ask ourselves whether we are happy as individuals, even though many people are gathered here, how many can say, "I am happy. I am eternally happy"? That is the question. Even though men and women are sitting together here, what every family, man, or woman desires is a happy family. They are hoping for and preparing for a happy family.

From that perspective, how many truly happy families are there? That is the issue. Broadly speaking, when we look at a nation or a people, America is a country that walks at the forefront of all material civilization in the world, but when we look at the sovereignty of this country or the entire population, are this country and its people truly happy? When we consider this question, there are many problems.

Currently, nearly 4 billion people live around the world, but are those nations, or individuals, or families happy? We know that this is a problematic situation. There may be great religious figures, rare philosophers in history, and scientists. However, can they truly bring happiness to the human world? No one has wished for that, and no one has failed to strive for it, but what we find in our current conditions is that there are more conditions of unhappiness than happiness.

Who is the master of happiness?

So, who is the master of happiness? Everyone, that is a serious question. When we ask who the master of happiness is, there is no one who can say, "I am the master of happiness." No one can claim, "This country is the master of happiness. This world is the master of happiness. This religion is the master of happiness." The assertion that "I must be happy" does not make one a master. It must be a passive position. It should be that the country must be happy, that a certain religion must fulfill the mission of achieving happiness.

From that perspective, when we ask who the master of happiness is, we do not know the master, and when we ask where the source of happiness is, we do not know the source, and seeking happiness itself seems foolish.

For a woman, a man can be the subject of happiness, and in a family, parents can be the subject of happiness. However, while that may be one aspect of our lives, through our entire lives, from an ideological or idealistic perspective, we find that it does not escape its limitations. Why? Because a wife thinks of her husband as the subject of her happiness, but that husband is also seeking happiness. Parents may seem to be the subjects of happiness in front of their children, but those same parents also need happiness and are in the position of seeking happiness.

Otherwise, the world will perish; we can conclude that there is no way to survive. Therefore, a prophet must come, right? “Yes.” You want that, and the people of the whole world want that, and God wants that, and the spirits in the spiritual world want that. 

Should such a person come or not? “They must come.” Are you confident in that answer? “Yes.” How? Because such a task remains, thankfully, there is a slogan that answers that task. That is, “The Messiah is coming, the Messiah. The Messiah is coming.” Then is the Messiah a philosopher or a prophet? “A prophet.” He is the king of prophets. (cheers, applause) Just saying that is good; if you meet him, it will be amazing! (laughs) 

Therefore, no matter what anyone says in the world, even if all the religions of the world perish, the time has come for a religion that clearly teaches that the Messiah must come. Now, do you prefer the Messiah to be a man or a woman? “A man.” If you ask women, they will say, “A woman! Men only use words like thieves.” (laughs) In Christianity, there is a saying in the Bible that “When the Messiah comes, He comes to conquer the world. He comes to judge.” Isn’t that right? You know that, right? So, did He only say that? There is also a saying that the Messiah comes to find a bride. There are these two sayings. Then which comes first, judging or finding a bride? Which comes first? “Finding a bride.” That’s right. Your answer is correct. First, you must find a bride. Then how will the judgment be made? How will it be judged? The first article is like this, the second article is like this, the third article is like this, and how will the judgment be made? What do you think? “Truth.” What is truth? Is it a man? A man. What kind of man? The Messiah! (applause) 

In the Bible, there is a saying, “I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me….” If Jesus is the truth, then that Jesus is a person, right? Then what is truth? When we ask what the truth itself is, it is a true person. Why does Jesus come as a bridegroom and need to find a bride? Because to be a true person, there must not only be a man but also a woman. That’s what it means. So, it is to establish a standard of true man and true woman. When true men and true women emerge, the false men and women must be filtered out. 

Then when a man is called the Lord of the Second Advent, the Messiah, how much percentage do you think you can be like that Messiah? Do you think you are 80% alike? How similar are you? Zero percent? (laughs) How much do you think you resemble him? Think about it. “I am 100% alike.” Raise your hand if you think so. Is there anyone like that? Can President Ford, being the President of the United States, say, “I am the President, so I am 100% like the Messiah”? “No.” (laughs) If he says “no,” what will happen? If you are an American citizen, you must say “yes.” Then what about the Pope? Is the Pope 100% alike? “No.” Then what about Billy Graham? Is he 100% alike? “No.” There is not a single person in the world who is 100% alike. There is none. Does the Pope know what percentage he is alike? Does Billy Graham know what percentage he is alike? That’s why the Messiah must come. He must come and compare. 

Then who knows that? Who knows? God knows. Therefore, it concludes that everyone must stand before the judgment seat. What is judgment? It is to measure whether it aligns with the constitution and laws or not. Isn’t that right? That is judgment. From that perspective, everyone must stand before the judgment seat. 

Then what is the most important thing to learn for a person? Is it more important to learn about the world, astronomy, and science, or is it more important to learn about people and God? “God.” Therefore, in the path of learning, what is the most precious and urgent issue for us? It is learning about God and understanding how humans came to be. This is the most important thing. 

What kind of man is that man? He is the Messiah. Then what teaches that? A true religion is one that clearly teaches God and properly teaches the Messiah. Such a religion is a true religion. Can you learn that in school? “No.” Then where? “Barrytown.” (laughs) Barrytown refers to that city. Then where is the true religion? You must search for religion, but what kind of religion is the true religion? That is the question. What is it? What was mentioned earlier? Truth. What is it? A true religion is a place where true people gather, a place that teaches how to become true people, and a place where true people are becoming true. That is the conclusion. 

Our Unification Church is what? Is the Unification Church a religion? Is it a school? “A religion.” It is a religion. However, now in places like NBC in America, there is so much controversy about Reverend Moon being a fake. When Americans go to Belvedere, Barrytown, and meet Koreans, they ask if they know Reverend Moon.
is. Now I've made a name for myself. "What's good? What's bad?" It's a big deal. 
(Laughter) I became famous without even realizing it, without even knowing it. Do you know how I became so famous? "Yes." Did I become famous in a good way or a bad way? "In a good way." (Laughter) Honestly, tell me, honestly. Let's be honest. "In a bad way." (Laughter) Right, in a bad way. 
So, is there anyone among you who thinks our teacher is a bad person? If so, raise your hand. "No." Are you all correct? "Yes." Even though there are more people in the entire United States who think I'm bad, am I a good person? "Yes." "Those people have never met Reverend Moon, but I have lived and I know..." That's how you should respond. That's why our claim is correct. We must assert that our claim is right. 
No matter how much the world makes noise, it doesn't matter. I don't even consider myself a problem. 
So, is it good or bad to oppose and complain? "It's bad." No, opposing makes you famous. Good advertising doesn't spread quickly, but bad advertising spreads fast. Everyone loves bad rumors. Why? Because they are on the side of evil Satan; the world of Satan loves that kind of thing. (Laughter) That's why it spreads quickly. First, it's good because it promotes us, and second, the more you oppose, the more you think, "These kids! In reality, it's like this..." and you become more united with the teacher. You cooperate and become more united with the teacher. So, the world tells you to oppose. Not just NBC, ABC, CBS, but all media should oppose. Instead, even a small doll-like girl can jump onto the world media stage and say, "What are you?" (Laughter) You step on countless media. So how powerful are you? How powerful are you? The stronger the world is, the stronger you become internally. In this sense, even if the teacher is opposed, I say, "Go ahead, go ahead." That's why it's okay to be opposed. So, is it good or bad to oppose? "It's good." 
When you pass by a neighborhood, the dogs in that neighborhood are bound to bark. It's the same thing. (Laughter) 
In America, I'm considered a strange person. Reverend Moon is a strange person, right? Look. Even senators and presidents in America cannot do what you all do. With complicated racial issues involving white, black, and yellow youth, an unexpected Asian person comes and sets up an interpreter, saying, "Do this." and everyone responds, "Yes." "Do that." and they respond, "Yes." If I say come, they come, and if I say go, they go. Isn't that strange? That's why the dogs are bound to bark. (Laughter) The dogs are bound to bark. So I think, "Bark away! The more the dog barks, the more its owner will come out to stop it." That's how I feel. So, I'm at peace. That's why I gain weight. I gain weight even while being opposed. 
This time, the incident involving someone named Wendy Helender is being pushed by famous newspapers like the New York Times and the Washington Post, and just like when President Nixon was supported, if it becomes a nationwide boom, we can immediately warn, "You must not become an American who imprisons innocent people." How wonderful is it to have material to warn about? Then the opposition will gradually decrease. However, I still think that the opposition must not disappear; I believe we need to receive more opposition, which is why I remain quiet. 
When a wrestler steps into the ring, it's exciting to knock down the opponent with a big "bang!" amidst the opposing crowd shouting, "Knock him down!" If you just sit quietly smoking a cigarette saying, "Let the two of them fight," where's the fun in that? Which is better? Is it better to do it quietly, or amidst opposition? Which is better? "It's better amidst opposition." That's what I like. I say to oppose quickly. Quickly... If reporters from newspapers are here today, don't go tell the newspaper president this. That way, they will oppose even more. (Laughter) Confident and capable people find it more enjoyable to be opposed. 
So, do you like believing in the Unification Church, or not? "Yes." Why? "Because it's exciting." (Laughter) Exciting? What's exciting? If Reverend Moon keeps making me work like this, making me suffer, isn't that exciting? You rascal! And you still like it? Well, then? "Yes." Oh, you crazy people! (Laughter. Applause) 
Your mothers and fathers think that opposing is right. They think it's right. (Laughter. Applause) Honestly, that's true. Shall we speak openly? "Yes." Why is it good? Why is it good? That's the question. What your mothers and fathers think is centered around themselves, while what we think is centered around the Messiah and God. That's why it's different. That's why it's good. (Laughter) It's different. So, we must stay until the end, and in the judgment time at the end, we must go through the Messiah and God to reach a place where we can pass, which is why we want to walk the path that can lead to passing. We know the highest teachings among the teachings of true religions, which is why you like it. This is how it becomes. 
Now, look. What position are you in? We are in the cosmic courtroom. God is the judge, and Jesus is the lawyer. The Lord who is coming is the lawyer. Then Satan is the prosecutor. We are standing in the courtroom. No matter how much Satan accuses, it doesn't matter. Right here, we are on our side. (Writing on the board while speaking) 
You must go through many trials and training to do great things. 
That's why I think that suffering for a day, a year, three years, or ten years is not a problem. It's not a problem. Therefore, the Unification Church develops the more it is opposed. The more others oppose, the stronger we become. 
That's why what's most frightening about joining the Unification Church? It's not making you work. Not making you work is the scariest thing. And not sending you out for evangelism is the scariest thing. Not making you do fundraising is the scariest thing, and not sending you out for evangelism is the scariest thing. Isn't that true? "Yes." Why is that? Look. I am different from others. I will build my own school, and I will build my own house, and I will create society with my own hands. My thoughts are different. 
Money, if I have money, what will I do? I have money to eat and live, and I have money to spend. I don't need to earn money even if I come to America. Why would I make such a fuss to earn money here? What is the biggest school in America? I want to create a school in heaven that is better than the best school in America. I think we should create a school that God loves more than Harvard University in America. If the Empire State Building is not in the name of God, we will buy the Empire State Building, which is the most beloved by America, to be in the name of God. (Cheers. Applause) We want to create the best. 
Then, will it take ten years to create the most famous school in the world, or three years? Considering God's prestige and the prestige of the Messiah who will come, what will we do? "In three years." In the name of God, in the name of the future Messiah, we will create the best in the world in the shortest period, one-third, one-fifth, or one-tenth of the time of other schools. Which one do you choose? The longest one or the shortest one? "The shortest one." (Applause) That's because you resemble me. You resemble me. (Laughter. Applause) 
Americans say, "Oh! That Oriental Reverend Moon came to American society and bought Belvedere in no time. He bought East Garden and bought something seven times the Columbia University Club! Should he create a seminary or a university...?" They say. I will buy a private jet, a jumbo jet. 
How about that? Does it make you feel bad? In the name of God, in the name of Reverend Moon... But does that mean I will just make you work and I will just play and eat? "No." I do bother you, right? That's right, isn't it? "No." The teacher has suffered more for God than you have, and throughout my life, I have endured all kinds of suffering and have not tired of standing at the forefront until now. If you became a teacher in the Unification Church, how long do you think you would endure? (Laughter) Try it! You oppose, you complain, there are all kinds of incidents. Not just anyone can take the position of a teacher in the Unification Church, except for Reverend Moon. Even if I don't want to, I do it. That's what's cool. That's what's cool. That's why it's worth it. 
Ladies, do you like that kind of man? "Yes." (Laughter) If I were a woman, I would want to marry a husband like Reverend Moon. I actually do that. (Laughter. Applause) I can do anything. There's nothing I can't do. Can I not exercise? Can I not do anything? There's nothing I can't do. If I decide to do something, it all becomes possible. Even if I were to steal, I would be the best at it. (Laughter) That's why I have the ability to guide you in many ways. I am trained. 
Think about it. Reverend Moon, who was born in a small Korea, a Reverend Moon with no name, came to America, which dominates the democratic world, and thought, "I will step on America and take hold of it. America must be moved." Do you think I came unprepared? Think about how much training I must have gone through. I am someone who has undergone that kind of training. I have experienced severe beatings in prison and have gone through all kinds of things. I am someone who knows both the bitter and sweet tastes of humanity. 
I realized that everything I encounter for one good purpose becomes a weapon and a bullet for the battles of the future. That's why I train you, who resemble me, to become like me. If you don't want to resemble me, then go away. Go away. Is there anyone who wants to leave? "Yes." Thank you. (Applause) 
So, what is the problem going forward? The title of today's message is "How Would You Answer If You Asked Me?" When we consider what we need to know among humans living in ignorance, we must recognize that knowing the Messiah and knowing God is the most precious thing. 
Knowing God and knowing the Messiah is the most precious thing. 
Now you don't have to think for yourself. You just have to follow. On the day you hold onto God and only hold onto the Messiah, who is the Son of God, when he follows you home, he will be welcomed the most in that house, and when he follows you to the country, he will be welcomed the most in that country, and when he goes to the world, he will be welcomed the most in the world, and when he goes to heaven, God will welcome him. You don't need to do anything else. 
When you meet the Messiah, when you see that Messiah, you will know what kind of person you are. The Messiah knows the way to go, knows what the future holds, knows what the family is like, knows what the country is like, knows what the world is like, knows what the spirit world is like, and knows everything as God knows it, which is why you will come to stand in a position where you can know as well. The more you follow, the more mysterious and interesting things will happen. Of course, there will be waves, but riding a boat that gently overcomes those high waves is much cooler. The things you do may seem strange and impossible, but if you look closely, they succeed beautifully and are truly amazing. How wonderful would that be? 
When you know and meet the Messiah, you will become a little Messiah, and you will be able to discern whether something good or bad will happen today, and the future will gradually become clearer. So, do we need the Messiah? "Yes." Does America need the Messiah? "The Messiah." Would you rather abandon America to receive the Messiah, or abandon the Messiah to protect America? "I would rather abandon America to receive the Messiah." Would you rather abandon all of humanity to receive the Messiah? "Yes." Then would you abandon God to receive the Messiah? "Yes." (Laughter) Answer clearly! "No." (Laughter) I would like to clarify this question, but I will hold back because I fear that people from established churches will say, "Oh! Reverend Moon's words until now have been good, but hearing the last words, it sounds like a cult..." "No." 
Now, since time is up, let's stop. If it's been two hours, it's enough, right? In America, the principle is to speak for 40 minutes, but it's already been two hours. So let's stop now. "No." I'm hungry. (Laughter) Reverend Moon is good because he is honest. He is honest. Isn't that right? "Yes." (Laughter) This morning, I honestly said, "Wouldn't it be great if I could talk for just one hour with my mother?" and there was a lot of debate. If you say to speak briefly, I speak long, and if you say to speak long, I speak briefly... (Laughter) But the impact remains the same. Now that two hours have passed, let's conclude. 
If you know God and the Messiah, that's all you need. What kind of person is Reverend Moon? Everything I have studied and worked for until now is not for anything else. It is to study the way to know God and the Messiah. Reverend Moon is not a philosopher. So what am I? I belong to the prophet club. Isn't that right? That's why, even while being opposed, they say, "Let's see what happens to Reverend Moon." Even so, I say, "If you oppose, what will you do? I am Reverend Moon!" That's how it is. You all feel the same, right? "Yes." Do you watch like the people of the world? "No." Then what will you do? Will you follow me, or will you go ahead of me? "I will go ahead." Then will I follow you? (Laughter) I said I would grab and pull you along, so pull me along. If you want to go ahead, you have to pull me along, right? (Laughter) If you let go, you will go somewhere else. 
Go out with the confidence that the Unification Church is a church that can unify religions. 
You have learned a lot since joining the Unification Church, right? "Yes." Now you can understand "How does God become, how does the world become, and how do we become?" The Unification Church knows how it will go and how it will become. Now, do you think the Unification Church will fail like established churches, or will it break through? What do you think? "It will break through." Why? How? Because you are here. Because there are young people, I am still here. It's because of you, or is it because of the teacher? "The teacher." I am old. I am old. Yes, I am old, but I am young enough not to lose to young people. Now, let's wrestle. (Laughter) I am young. That's why, even though I am old, I am guiding young people.
So the Unification Church is moving forward.  
The Unification Church can unite the five races into one. How? Because I can marry people as I please. No one else in world history can do that. Do you acknowledge that? "Yes." Because I can freely unite white people with black people, white people with yellow people, and yellow people with black people, there is a great possibility of truly uniting the world. How many of you believe that this is possible? No need to ask. That's why you have come well into the Unification Church. "Yes." Those who believe you have come well, raise your hands. However, it is difficult to go well. Do you want to go well or not? "We will go well."  
Now you all understand. You know how individuals become, how families become, how nations become, and how we should go. You understand how nations will become, how the world will become, and how the Kingdom of Heaven will become. The person known as Teacher Moon of the Unification Church is not a philosopher but is not an ignorant person either. He is someone who knows everything. You all need to know everything as well. This is theoretical. It means not believing blindly. In that sense, while you may think of the Unification Church as vague, you must understand that it is laying a scientific foundation in today's society.  
Everyone, what is science? Science starts from hypotheses. If the results match through experiments, it is called scientific. The Unification Church is even more certain than that. It is not a hypothesis. Because it can have experimental results based on content, I know that it can become a religion that can move. I know the path I must take clearly. I also know how the world will become in the future. Do you understand that? Even if I try to explain it to you, you wouldn't know. Only I know that. Only God and I know that. Therefore, the teacher can engage with any philosopher from a theoretical perspective and can see everything about the world of mystery clearly. I am an expert in the spiritual world. (Laughter) If I were to teach you such things, you would try to run away in the opposite direction, so I do not teach them.  
So now, knowing this amazing fact that the Unification Church can unify churches and religions, and knowing how life should proceed in the future, you must pave the highway to the bright world. Thus, learn to drive and think, "I am the one who is excitedly driving towards my destination in a good Lincoln limousine from the morning." That feels good. So learn to drive. Even if there are persecutions along the way, let's go while humming a tune. That's how we should go. That’s why we are not ignorant people, but knowledgeable people, and that makes us happy. Take care. (Applause)
